let rec pack_consecutive_duplicates x =
  match x with
  | [] -> []
  | x::xs ->
      let y = x::xs in
      let z = pack_consecutive_duplicates y in
      let w = x::z in
      w
in
let rec pack_consecutive_duplicates_rec x =
  match x with
  | [] -> []
  | x::xs ->
      let y = x::xs in
      let z = pack_consecutive_duplicates_rec y in
      let w = x::z in
      w
